  355→func (s *Service) getFallbackStrategyFor(provider string) (ssosettings.FallbackStrategy, bool) {\n   356→\tfor _, strategy := range s.fbStrategies {\n   357→\t\tif strategy.IsMatch(provider) {\n   358→\t\t\treturn strategy, true\n   359→\t\t}\n   360→\t}\n   361→\treturn nil, false\n   362→}\n   363→\n   364→func (s *Service) encryptSecrets(ctx context.Context, settings map[string]any) (map[string]any, error) {\n   365→\tresult := deepCopyMap(settings)\n   366→\tconfigs := getConfigMaps(result)\n   367→\n   368→\tfor _, config := range configs {\n   369→\t\tfor k, v := range config {\n   370→\t\t\tif IsSecretField(k) && v != \"\" {\n   371→\t\t\t\tstrValue, ok := v.(string)\n   372→\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n   373→\t\t\t\t\treturn result, fmt.Errorf(\"failed to encrypt %s setting because it is not a string: %v\", k, v)\n   374→\t\t\t\t}\n   375→\n   376→\t\t\t\tencryptedSecret, err := s.secrets.Encrypt(ctx, []byte(strValue), secrets.WithoutScope())\n   377→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   378→\t\t\t\t\treturn result, err\n   379→\t\t\t\t}\n   380→\t\t\t\tconfig[k] = base64.RawStdEncoding.EncodeToString(encryptedSecret)\n   381→\t\t\t}\n   382→\t\t}\n   383→\t}\n   384→\n   385→\treturn result, nil\n   386→}\n   387→\n   388→func (s *Service) Run(ctx context.Context) error {\n   389→\tinterval := s.cfg.SSOSettingsReloadInterval\n   390→\tif interval == 0 {\n   391→\t\treturn nil\n   392→\t}\n   393→\n   394→\tticker := time.NewTicker(interval)\n   395→\n   396→\t// start a background process for reloading the SSO settings for all providers at a fixed interval\n   397→\t// it is useful for high availability setups running multiple Grafana instances\n   398→\tfor {\n   399→\t\tselect {\n   400→\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n   401→\t\t\ts.doReload(ctx)\n   402→\n   403→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   404→\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n   405→\t\t}\n   406→\t}\n   407→}\n   408→\n   409→func (s *Service) doReload(ctx context.Context) {\n   410→\ts.logger.Debug(\"reloading SSO Settings for all providers\")\n   411→\n   412→\tsettingsList, err := s.List(ctx)\n   413→\tif err != nil {\n   414→\t\ts.logger.Error(\"failed to fetch SSO Settings for all providers\", \"err\", err)\n   415→\t\treturn\n   416→\t}\n   417→\n   418→\tfor provider, connector := range s.reloadables {\n   419→\t\tsettings := getSettingByProvider(provider, settingsList)\n   420→\n   421→\t\tif settings == nil || len(settings.Settings) == 0 {\n   422→\t\t\ts.logger.Warn(\"SSO Settings is empty\", \"provider\", provider)\n   423→\t\t\tcontinue\n   424→\t\t}\n   425→\n   426→\t\terr = connector.Reload(ctx, *settings)\n   427→\t\tif err != nil {\n   428→\t\t\ts.metrics.reloadFailures.WithLabelValues(provider).Inc()\n   429→\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"failed to reload SSO Settings\", \"provider\", provider, \"err\", err)\n   430→\t\t\tcontinue\n   431→\t\t}\n   432→\t}\n   433→}\n   434→\n   435→// mergeSSOSettings merges the settings from the database with the system settings\n   436→// Required because it is possible that the user has configured some of the settings (current Advanced OAuth settings)\n   437→// and the rest of the settings have to be loaded from the system settings\n   438→func (s *Service) mergeSSOSettings(dbSettings, systemSettings *models.SSOSettings) *models.SSOSettings {\n   439→\tif dbSettings == nil {\n   440→\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"No SSO Settings found in the database, using system settings\")\n   441→\t\treturn systemSettings\n   442→\t}\n   443→\n   444→\ts.logger.Debug(\"Merging SSO Settings\", \"dbSettings\", removeSecrets(dbSettings.Settings), \"systemSettings\", removeSecrets(systemSettings.Settings))\n   445→\n   446→\tresult := &models.SSOSettings{\n   447→\t\tProvider: dbSettings.Provider,\n   448→\t\tSource:   dbSettings.Source,\n   449→\t\tSettings: mergeSettings(dbSettings.Settings, systemSettings.Settings),\n   450→\t\tCreated:  dbSettings.Created,\n   451→\t\tUpdated:  dbSettings.Updated,\n   452→\t}\n   453→\n   454→\treturn result\n   455→}\n   456→\n   457→func (s *Service) decryptSecrets(ctx context.Context, settings map[string]any) (map[string]any, error) {\n   458→\tconfigs := getConfigMaps(settings)\n   459→\n   460→\tfor _, config := range configs {\n   461→\t\tfor k, v := range config {\n   462→\t\t\tif IsSecretField(k) && v != \"\" {\n   463→\t\t\t\tstrValue, ok := v.(string)\n   464→\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n   465→\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.FromContext(ctx).Error(\"Failed to parse secret value, it is not a string\", \"key\", k)\n   466→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"secret value is not a string\")\n   467→\t\t\t\t}\n   468→\n   469→\t\t\t\tdecoded, err := base64.RawStdEncoding.DecodeString(strValue)\n   470→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   471→\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.FromContext(ctx).Error(\"Failed to decode secret string\", \"err\", err, \"value\")\n   472→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   473→\t\t\t\t}\n   474→\n   475→\t\t\t\tdecrypted, err := s.secrets.Decrypt(ctx, decoded)\n   476→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   477→\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.FromContext(ctx).Error(\"Failed to decrypt secret\", \"err\", err)\n   478→\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   479→\t\t\t\t}\n   480→\n   481→\t\t\t\tconfig[k] = string(decrypted)\n   482→\t\t\t}\n   483→\t\t}\n   484→\t}\n   485→\n   486→\treturn settings, nil\n   487→}\n   488→\n   489→func (s *Service) isProviderConfigurable(provider string) bool {\n   490→\tenabled, ok := s.configurableProviders[provider]\n   491→\treturn ok && enabled\n   492→}\n   493→\n   494→// removeSecrets removes all the secrets from the map and replaces them with a redacted password\n   495→// and returns a new map\n   496→func removeSecrets(settings map[string]any) map[string]any {\n   497→\tresult := deepCopyMap(settings)\n   498→\tconfigs := getConfigMaps(result)\n   499→\n   500→\tfor _, config := range configs {\n   501→\t\tfor k, v := range config {\n   502→\t\t\tval, ok := v.(string)\n   503→\t\t\tif ok && val != \"\" && IsSecretField(k) {\n   504→\t\t\t\tconfig[k] = setting.RedactedPassword\n   505→\t\t\t}\n   506→\t\t}\n   507→\t}\n   508→\treturn result\n   509→}\n   510→\n   511→// getConfigMaps returns a list of maps that may contain secrets\n   512→func getConfigMaps(settings map[string]any) []map[string]any {\n   513→\t// always include the main settings map\n   514→\tresult := []map[string]any{settings}\n   515→\n   516→\t// for LDAP include settings for each server\n   517→\tif config, ok := settings[\"config\"].(map[string]any); ok {\n   518→\t\tif servers, ok := config[\"servers\"].([]any); ok {\n   519→\t\t\tfor _, server := range servers {\n   520→\t\t\t\tif serverSettings, ok := server.(map[string]any); ok {\n   521→\t\t\t\t\tresult = append(result, serverSettings)\n   522→\t\t\t\t}\n   523→\t\t\t}\n   524→\t\t}\n   525→\t}\n   526→\n   527→\treturn result\n   528→}\n   529→\n   530→// mergeSettings merges two maps in a way that the values from the first map are preserved\n   531→// and the values from the second map are added only if they don't exist in the first map\n   532→// or if they contain empty URLs.\n   533→func mergeSettings(storedSettings, systemSettings map[string]any) map[string]any {\n   534→\tsettings := make(map[string]any)\n   535→\n   536→\tfor k, v := range storedSettings {\n   537→\t\tsettings[k] = v\n   538→\t}\n   539→\n   540→\tfor k, v := range systemSettings {\n   541→\t\tif _, ok := settings[k]; !ok {\n   542→\t\t\tif isMergingAllowed(k) {\n   543→\t\t\t\tsettings[k] = v\n   544→\t\t\t}\n   545→\t\t} else if isURL(k) && isEmptyString(settings[k]) {\n   546→\t\t\t// Overwrite all URL settings from the DB containing an empty string with their value\n   547→\t\t\t// from the system settings. This fixes an issue with empty auth_url, api_url and token_url\n   548→\t\t\t// from the DB not being replaced with their values defined in the system settings for\n   549→\t\t\t// the Google provider.\n   550→\t\t\tsettings[k] = v\n   551→\t\t}\n   552→\t}\n   553→\n   554→\treturn settings\n   555→}\n   556→\n   557→// isMergingAllowed returns true if the field provided can be merged from the system settings.\n   558→// It won't allow SAML fields that are part of a group of settings to be merged from system settings\n   559→// because the DB settings already contain one valid setting from each group.\n   560→func isMergingAllowed(fieldName string) bool {\n   561→\tforbiddenMergePatterns := []string{\"certificate\", \"private_key\", \"idp_metadata\"}\n   562→\n   563→\tfor _, v := range forbiddenMergePatterns {\n   564→\t\tif strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(fieldName), strings.ToLower(v)) {\n   565→\t\t\treturn false\n   566→\t\t}\n   567→\t}\n   568→\treturn true\n   569→}\n   570→\n   571→// mergeSecrets returns a new map with the current value for secrets that have not been updated\n   572→func mergeSecrets(settings map[string]any, storedSettings map[string]any) (map[string]any, error) {\n   573→\tsettingsWithSecrets := deepCopyMap(settings)\n   574→\tnewConfigs := getConfigMaps(settingsWithSecrets)\n   575→\tstoredConfigs := getConfigMaps(storedSettings)\n s.cfg.SSOSettingsReloadInterval\n\tif interval == 0 {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tticker := time.NewTicker(interval)\n\n\t// start a background process for reloading the SSO settings for all providers at a fixed interval\n\t// it is useful for high availability setups running multiple Grafana instances\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase <-ticker.C:\n\t\t\ts.doReload(ctx)\n\n\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n\t\t\treturn ctx.Err()\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (s *Service) doReload(ctx context.Context) {\n\ts.logger.Debug(\"reloading SSO Settings for all providers\")\n\n\tsettingsList, err := s.List(ctx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\ts.logger.Error(\"failed to fetch SSO Settings for all providers\", \"err\", err)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\tfor provider, connector := range s.reloadables {\n\t\tsettings := getSettingByProvider(provider, settingsList)\n\n\t\tif settings == nil || len(settings.Settings) == 0 {\n\t\t\ts.logger.Warn(\"SSO Settings is empty\", \"provider\", provider)\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\terr = connector.Reload(ctx, *settings)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\ts.metrics.reloadFailures.WithLabelValues(provider).Inc()\n\t\t\ts.logger.Error(\"failed to reload SSO Settings\", \"provider\", provider, \"err\", err)\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\n// mergeSSOSettings merges the settings from the database with the system settings\n// Required because it is possible that the user has configured some of the settings (current Advanced OAuth settings)\n// and the rest of the settings have to be loaded from the system settings\nfunc (s *Service) systemSettings.Settings),\n\t\tCreated:  dbSettings.Created,\n\t\tUpdated:  dbSettings.Updated,\n\t}\n\n\treturn result\n}\n\nfunc (s *Service) decryptSecrets(ctx context.Context, settings map[string]any) (map[string]any, error) {\n\tconfigs := getConfigMaps(settings)\n\n\tfor _, config := range configs {\n\t\tfor k, v := range config {\n\t\t\tif IsSecretField(k) && v != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\tstrValue, ok := v.(string)\n\t\t\t\tif !ok {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.FromContext(ctx).Error(\"Failed to parse secret value, it is not a string\", \"key\", k)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"secret value is not a string\")\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tdecoded, err := base64.RawStdEncoding.DecodeString(strValue)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.FromContext(ctx).Error(\"Failed to decode secret string\", \"err\", err, \"value\")\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tdecrypted, err := s.secrets.Decrypt(ctx, decoded)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\ts.logger.FromContext(ctx).Error(\"Failed to decrypt secret\", \"err\", err)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tconfig[k] = string(decrypted)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn settings, nil\n}\n\nfunc (s *Service) isProviderConfigurable(provider string) bool {\n\tenabled, ok := s.configurableProviders[provider]\n\treturn ok && enabled\n}\n\n// removeSecrets removes all the secrets from the map and replaces them with a redacted password\n// and returns a new map\nfunc removeSecrets(settings map[string]any) map[string]any {\n\tresult := deepCopyMap(settings)\n\tconfigs := getConfigMaps(result)\n\n\tfor _, config := range configs {\n\t\tfor k, v := range config {\n\t\t\tval, ok := v.(string)\n\t\t\tif ok && val != \"\" && IsSecretField(k) {\n\t\t\t\tconfig[k] = setting.RedactedPassword\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn result\n}\n\n// getConfigMaps returns a list of maps that may contain secrets\nfunc getConfigMaps(settings map[string]any) []map[string]any {\n\t// always include the main settings map\n\tresult := []map[string]any{settings}\n\n\t// for LDAP include settings for each server\n\tif config, ok := settings[\"config\"].(map[string]any); ok {\n\t\tif servers, ok := config[\"servers\"].([]any); ok {\n\t\t\tfor _, server := range servers {\n\t\t\t\tif serverSettings, ok := server.(map[string]any); ok {\n\t\t\t\t\tresult = append(result, serverSettings)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn result\n}\n\n// mergeSettings merges two maps in a way that the values from the first map are preserved\n// and the values from the second map are added only if they don't exist in the first map\n// or if they contain empty URLs.\nfunc mergeSettings(storedSettings, systemSettings map[string]any) map[string]any {\n\tsettings := make(map[string]any)\n\n\tfor k, v := range storedSettings {\n\t\tsettings[k] = v\n\t}\n\n\tfor k, v := range systemSettings {\n\t\tif _, ok := settings[k]; !ok {\n\t\t\tif isMergingAllowed(k) {\n\t\t\t\tsettings[k] = v\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t} else if isURL(k) && isEmptyString(settings[k]) {\n\t\t\t// Overwrite all URL settings from the DB This fixes an issue with empty auth_url, api_url and token_url\n\t\t\t// from the DB not being replaced with their values defined in the system settings for\n\t\t\t// the Google provider.\n\t\t\tsettings[k] = v\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn settings\n}\n\n// isMergingAllowed returns true if the field provided can be merged from the system settings.\n// It won't allow SAML fields that are part of a group of settings to be merged from system settings\n// because the DB settings already contain one valid setting from each group.\nfunc isMergingAllowed(fieldName string) bool {\n\tforbiddenMergePatterns := []string{\"certificate\", \"private_key\", \"idp_metadata\"}\n\n\tfor _, v := range forbiddenMergePatterns {\n\t\tif strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(fieldName), strings.ToLower(v)) {\n\t\t\treturn false\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// mergeSecrets returns a new map with the current value for secrets that have not been updated\nfunc mergeSecrets(settings make(map[string]any)\n\tfor _, m := range maps {\n\t\tfor k, v := range m {\n\t\t\tresult[k] = v\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn result\n}\n\n// IsSecretField returns true if the SSO settings field provided is a secret\nfunc IsSecretField(fieldName string) bool {\n\tsecretFieldPatterns := []string{\"secret\", \"private\", \"certificate\", \"password\", \"client_key\"}\n\n\tfor _, v := range secretFieldPatterns {\n\t\tif strings.Contains(strings.ToLower(fieldName), strings.ToLower(v)) {\n\t\t\treturn true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn false\n}\n\nfunc isURL(fieldName string) bool {\n\treturn setting.RedactedPassword\n}\n\nfunc deepCopyMap(settings map[string]any) map[string]any {\n\tnewSettings := make(map[string]any)\n\n\tfor key, value := range settings {\n\t\tswitch v := value.(type) {\n\t\tcase map[string]any:\n\t\t\tnewSettings[key] = deepCopyMap(v)\n\t\tcase []any:\n\t\t\tnewSettings[key] = deepCopySlice(v)\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tnewSettings[key] = value\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn newSettings\n}\n\nfunc deepCopySlice(s []any) []any {\n\tnewSlice := make([]any, len(s))\n\n\tfor i, value := range s {\n\t\tswitch v := value.(type) {\n\t\tcase map[string]any:\n\t\t\tnewSlice[i] = []*models.SSOSettings) {\n\ts.cacheMutex.Lock()\n\tdefer s.cacheMutex.Unlock()\n\n\ts.cachedSSOSettings = settings\n}\n\nfunc (s *Service) updateCachedSSOSettings(provider string, settings definitions are in `errors.go`\\n- Fallback strategies are implemented in `strategies/` (oauth_strategy.go, ldap_strategy.go, saml_strategy.go) to load settings from configuration files\\n- Validation endpoints: GET/PUT/DELETE for provider settings and GET for listing all settings\\n- Each endpoint is protected with access control middleware using `ac.EvalPermission` with `OAuthInfo` from SSO settings and use it to configure their OAuth flow parameters\\n\\n**Layer 4: Access Control and DI Registration**\\nAccess control is defined in `pkg/services/accesscontrol/`:\\n- `EvalAuthenticationSettings` for SAML/LDAP and `OauthSettingsEvaluator` for OAuth providers\\n- `roles.go` defines role-based access control configurations\\n\\nDependency injection is wired in
